	<body>
		<category name="ThaCampin'Dutchpack">
			<category name="Description">
				<comment>By Aaron0000</comment>
				<comment>Replaces a large number of items in the game with ports and interpretations of ThaCampin'Dutchman's arsenal from Borderlands 1.</comment>
				<comment>Notes;</comment>
				<comment>Nothing is enabled by default. Toggle on what you want.</comment>
				<comment>Some items have different options as to what item should be replaced. Pick and choose.</comment>
				<comment>One of the items in this mod (Thermogenesis) uses a hotfix. Be sure to merge this mod with your main patch file.</comment>
			</category>
			<category name="Individual Item Descriptions">
				<category name="Weapons">
					<category name="Bandit Weapons">
						<category name="Dolos">
							<comment>Significantly increased pellet count, almost non-existent bullet speed. Increased critical hit damage.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Boganella by default, but can also replace Sledge's Shotgun instead.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Equuleus">
							<comment>Functions like a Revolver from Borderlands 1. Consumes three ammo per shot, increased magazine size.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Zim.</comment>
							<comment>Note; Allows the Zim to spawn in elements other than corrosive. Non-cryo Zims will be deleted if the mod isn't run.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Hawk">
							<comment>No recoil. Increased accuracy.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Sledge's Shotgun by default, but can also replace the Boganella instead.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Sickle">
							<comment>High fire rate. Fires in the shape of a sickle.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Boganella (uses Cyber Eagle firing mode).</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Traitor">
							<comment>x4 projectile count, very high fire reate, reduced accuracy, massize magazine size. Shooting once will attempt to empty the entire magazine of ammo.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Meat Grinder.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Vulcan Fury">
							<comment>Incredible fire rate and magazine size. Minimal accuracy, slow projectile speed.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Fusillade.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Zodiac">
							<comment>x12 projectile count, reduced damage per projectile. Massive magazine size. Consumes two ammo per shot.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Badaboom.</comment>
						</category>
					</category>
					<category name="Dahl Weapons">
						<category name="Altair">
							<comment>x3 projectiles, reduced damage per projectile.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Wet Week.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Barracuda">
							<comment>Dual element - Shock Bullet, Explosive splash. Rounds twist in flight, as well as ricochet off surfaces. Increased fire rate. Shock only.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Major Tom.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Komodo">
							<comment>Four-round burst-fire outside of scopes. Divides into multiple rounds on impact that ricochet multiple times. Increased elemental damage and chance. Corrosive only.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Blowfly.</comment>
						</category>
					</category>
					<category name="Hyperion Weapons">
						<category name="Agonizer">
							<comment>Explodes on contact with an enemy, penetrates enemies.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Logan's gun.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Hitman">
							<comment>Impeccable accuracy, high damage, low fire rate.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Fremington's Edge by default, or Invader.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Wildfire">
							<comment>Incendiary only. Increased elemental effects. Has a unique firing pattern.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Heartbreaker.</comment>
							<comment>Note; Enables Heartbreaker to spawn with sights. Sighted Heartbreakers will be deleted if you don't run the mod.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Vanquish">
							<comment>x2 projectiles. Reduced damage per projectile. Increased critical hit damage</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Fatale.</comment>
							<comment>Note; Enables Fatale to spawn with all elements. Non-Cryo Fatales will be deleted if this mod is not run.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Black Death">
							<comment>Creates a veritable hell of bullets upon ricohetting off a surface.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Viral Marketer.</comment>
							<comment>Note; In order to launch the child projectiles, I had to take the firing mode of the Shotgun Fibber (and made the barrel use a normal firing mode as well ad adjusted the stats of the barrel to fix it). Any mod that uses that firing mode is going to conflict.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Fusillation">
							<comment>Consumes 6 ammo per shot. Increased critical hit damage, reduced fire rate. Fires a large swath of projectiles.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Black Snake.</comment>
							<comment>Note; Enables the Black Snake to spawn in all elements. Non-Corrosive Black Snakes will be deleted if the mod is not run.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Oneshot">
							<comment>Extremely high damage, critical hit damage, and accuracy. Extrememly low fire rate and reload speed. Magazine size of 1. Consumes 5 ammo per shot. Only spawns with Hyperion parts.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Invader by default, but can also replace Fremington's Edge instead.</comment>
						</category>
					</category>
					<category name="Jakobs Weapons">
						<category name="Cricket">
							<comment>High knockback.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Smasher by default, but can also replace the Maggieinstead.</comment>

							<comment>x2 projectiles. Ricochets once.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Skullmasher.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Quash">
							<comment>High stats across the board, especially high magazine size. No sight. Has a two-round burst-fire when aiming down scopes.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces the Razorback.</comment>
							<comment>Note; There are two version of the Razorback replacer. One for use with the Unofficial Community Patch (on by default), and the other for standard Razorback.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Sawed-Off">
							<comment>High projectile count, increased damage. Minimal accuracy, magazine size of 2. Consumes 2 ammo per shot. Projectiles had a very short life span.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Striker.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Triple">
							<comment>Burst-fires three shots in rapid succession.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Maggie by default, but can also replace the Smasher instead.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Railgun">
							<comment>High damage and critical hit damage. Fires E-Tech projectiles. Consumes 2 ammo per shot.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Razorback.</comment>
							<comment>Note; Forces the Razorback to spawn with a scope. Scoped Razorbacks will be deleted if this mod is not run.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Wiseguy">
							<comment>The answer to everything.</comment>
							<comment>Always spawns with no accessory and a Jakobs grip.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Striker.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Boneduster">
							<comment>Magazine size is always four. Fires a large amount of invisible projectiles. High knockback and recoil. Zooming in and firing will fire an incendiary charge shot that consumes four ammo per shot. Always spawns with no sight.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Striker.</comment>
							<comment>Note; To achieve the charge shot effect, it uses and modifies the Badaboom's firing mode, affecting any mods that use it. If you aren't using a mod that replaces the Badaboom, use the Badaboom fixes included in the Boneduster areas to make the Badaboom function normally.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Moneyshot">
							<comment>Consumes 4 ammo per shot. Fires in the shape of a $ sign.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Striker.</comment>
						</category>

							<comment>Explosive only. Ricochets upon hitting a surface.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Chere-Amie.</comment>
							<comment>Note; Forces the Chere-Amie to spawn without an elemental part. Will remain as such even if the mod is not run. Does not affect existing Chere-Amies.</comment>
						</category>

							<comment>Consumes 2 ammo per shot, boosted elemental damage and chance. Incendiary only.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Hard Reboot.</comment>

							<comment>Replaces Magma.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Salvation">
							<comment>Heals allies when shooting them. Produces transfusion orbs upon shooting enemies. Passively restores health and ammunition. Actual damage to enemies is splash only.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Probe.</comment>
						</category>
						<category name="Thermogenesis">
							<comment>Consumes 5 ammo per shot. Fires a powerful, slow-moving laser that erupts 8 times upon striking a surface. Slow fire rate, massively increased burn damage and chance.</comment>
							<comment>Replaces Cryophobia.</comment>
							<comment>Note; This weapon uses the Logan's Gun projectile to achieve the erupting effect. Either use a Logan's Gun weapon replacer when using this weapon, or avoid using the Logan's Gun.</comment>
						</category>
